	country = SOV

	trigger = { atwar = no  }

	name = "1936年的苏联经济 "
	desc = "第二个五年计划已经执行了三年多，经济战线上呈现出可喜的成 果。据中央计划委员会统计显示，截止1935年底苏联的工业总产 值已经超过了法、英、德，仅次于美国，位居世界第二位。同时 ，最高苏维埃向全国发出号召――五年计划四年完成！得到了广 大工农群众的热烈响应。 "
	style = 2
	picture = "kelimulin"

	date = { day = 4 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 7
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = january year = 1936 }

	action_a = {
		name = "为共产主义事业而奋斗！ "
		command = { type = dissent value = -2 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 1107005
	country = SOV
	random = no
  
	trigger = { random = 50 atwar = no }

	name = "斯达汉诺夫运动 "
	desc = "1935年8月31日，年轻的煤矿工人斯达汉诺夫，改进掘煤方法，在 一个工作日内采煤102吨，超过普通工作日生产定额的13倍，成为 轰动一时的新闻。9月8日，他又刷新了纪录，一个工作日采煤175 吨。最高苏维埃政府抓住这一典型，加以总结推广，很快就在全 国各行业掀起以掌握新技术、改进旧工艺，提高生产率为目标的 ‘斯达汉诺夫运动’，体现了苏联人民为国家工业化而忘我工作 ，积极进取的精神，有力地推动了社会主义的建设事业。 "
	style = 0
	picture = "sidahannuofu"

	date = { day = 5 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 5
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = january year = 1937 }

	action_a = {
		name = "为共产主义事业而奋斗！ "
		command = { type = dissent value = -1 }
		command = { type = industrial_modifier which = total value = 2 }
		command = { type = research_mod value = 5 } 
	}
}

event = {
	id = 88
	random = no
	country = SOV

	decision = { war = { country = SOV country = GER } }

	decision_trigger = { 
		OR = {												
			NOT = {	control = { province = 3570 data = SOV }}
			NOT = {	control = { province = 237 data = SOV }}
			NOT = {	control = { province = 4095 data = SOV }}
		}													
	}
		
	trigger = {
		war = { country = SOV country = GER }													
		OR = {												
			NOT = {	control = { province = 3570 data = SOV }}
			NOT = {	control = { province = 237 data = SOV }}
			NOT = {	control = { province = 4095 data = SOV }}
		}													
	}
	
	name = "顿涅茨决堤 "
	desc = “第聂伯河大坝，完工于１９３２年，是欧洲最大的水利设置，也是斯大林时代的象征。当敌军进入顿涅兹盆地时，俄军炸毁了第 聂伯河大坝，导致了大规模的水灾和毁灭。 ”
	style = 0
	picture = "donetz_flood"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1940 }
	offset = 5
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1944 }

	action_a = {
		ai_chance = 95
		name = EVT_88_ACTA
		command = { type = dissent value = 2 }
		command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 235 value = -50 } 
		command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 236 value = -50 } 
		command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 234 value = -50 } 
		command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 250 value = -50 } 
		command = { type = set_ground which = 235 value = muddy } 
		command = { type = set_ground which = 236 value = muddy } 
		command = { type = set_ground which = 234 value = muddy } 
		command = { type = set_ground which = 250 value = muddy } 
	}
	action_b = {
		ai_chance = 5
		name = EVT_88_ACTB
		command = { } # no effects
	}
}

#########################################################################
#  Axis minor states switch sides (ROM) (Edited by 兰々)
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 60
	random = no
	country = ROM

	name = "改弦易辙--罗马尼亚试图投降 "
	desc = EVT_60_DESC
	picture = "minor"
	style = 0

	trigger = {
		alliance = { country = GER country = rom }	
		AND = {							
		        control = { province = 424 data = SOV }	
			lost_national = { country = rom value = 65 }								
		}												# BHT1.5
	}

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1942 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action_a = {
		ai_chance = 95
		name = EVT_60_ACTA
		command = { type = end_puppet }
		command = { type = leave_alliance }
		command = { type = set_relation which = GER value = -50 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 63 }
	}
	action_b = {
		ai_chance = 5
		name = EVT_60_ACTB
		command = { type = dissent value = 5 }
		command = { type = domestic which = defense_lobby value = 1 }
	}
}
